Aadhaar Aadhaar law it to by Through an amendment enacted in 2019 to the (Targeted Delivery of Financial and Other Subsidies, Benefits and Services) Act, 2016, was provided under section 4(4) of the Act that entities may be allowed to perform authentication if the Unique Identification Authority of is that the requesting entity is compliant with standards of privacy and security specified by regulations and is permitted by to authentication services or seeks authentication for prescribed Pursuant to this amendment, the said purposes were prescribed by the Authentication for Good Governance (Social Innovation, Knowledge) Rules, 2020. These rules provided that authentication requesting entities may be allowed in the interest of good governance, preventing leakage of public funds, promoting ease of living of residents and enabling better access services for for the purposes of of digital platforms ensure good governance, prevention of dissipation of social enablement of innovation the spread of them
